              <a href="about">
              </a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="col-md-6 slider__slide__text">
             <a href="about">
              <p>
               We empower and support organisations and individuals in and through the use of ICTs to contribute to equitable human development, social justice and environmental sustainability.
              </p>
             </a>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div>
          <div>
           <div class="slider__slide">
            <div class="col-md-6">
             <div style="background: url(https://www.apc.org/sites/default/files/DSC02370_2.JPG ) center;background-size: cover;height:100%; min-height: 400px;">
              <a href="https://www.apc.org/en/about">
              </a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="col-md-6 slider__slide__text">
             <a href="https://www.apc.org/en/about">
              <p>
               Our vision is for people to use and shape the internet and digital technologies to create a just and sustainable world, leading to greater care for ourselves, each other and the earth.
              </p>
             </a>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="row">
         <div class="col-md-12">
          <ul class="slider__navigation">
          </ul>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </section>

            <div class="col-sm-7 col-md-7 col-custom-sm-7">
             <a class="block__latest_news__item__title" href="/en/news/engagemedias-pretty-good-podcast-boosting-asia-pacific-voices-west-dominated-tech-discourse">
              EngageMedia's Pretty Good Podcast: Boosting Asia-Pacific voices in West-dominated tech discourse
             </a>
             <span class="block__latest_news__item__meta">
              <span>
               17 March 2021
              </span>
              By EngageMedia
             </span>
             <p class="block__latest_news__item__excerpt">
              The COVID-19 pandemic spurred on existing debates and developments on privacy, government surveillance and data monetisation. But what do all these mean for the Asia-Pacific, the region where most of the worlds population lives but whose voices are often overlooked in global tech discourse?
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>

            <div class="col-sm-7 col-md-7 col-custom-sm-7">
             <a class="block__latest_news__item__title" href="/en/news/racism-and-incitement-index-2020-increase-racism-and-incitement-against-palestinians-and-arabs">
              Racism and Incitement Index 2020: The Increase in racism and incitement against Palestinians and Arabs during the pandemic
             </a>
             <span class="block__latest_news__item__meta">
              <span>
               17 March 2021
              </span>
              By 7amleh - The Arab Center for the Advancement of Social Media
             </span>
             <p class="block__latest_news__item__excerpt">
              The results of 7amleh's Index of Racism and Incitement in Israeli Social Networks during the year 2020 showed an increase in violent discourse towards Arabs by 16% over the year 2019, with 1 out of every 10 posts about Palestinians and Arabs in 2020 containing violent speech.
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>

             <a class="block__latest_news__item__title" href="/en/news/india-tech-firms-should-uphold-privacy-free-speech">
              India: Tech firms should uphold privacy, free speech
             </a>
             <span class="block__latest_news__item__meta">
              <span>
               15 March 2021
              </span>
              By APC and others
             </span>
             <p class="block__latest_news__item__excerpt">
              The Indian government has taken various measures that violate free expression and privacy rights in response to growing international criticism of its handling of the farmers protests, targeting critics of the authorities and supporters of the protests.
             </p>

     <section class="block block-views clearfix" id="block-views-projects-home-feature">
      <!-- block__projects -->
      <section class="block__projects">
       <div class="container">
        <div class="row">
         <div class="col-xs-12">
          <h2>
           <a class="block__title" href="/en/projects">
            <h2>
             Projects
            </h2>
           </a>
          </h2>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="row">
         <div class="block__projects__slick">
          <div class="col-md-4">
           <div class="block__projects__item">
            <a href="/en/project/connecting-unconnected-supporting-community-networks-and-other-community-based-connectivity">
             <img alt="Connecting the Unconnected: Supporting community networks and other community-based connectivity initiatives" class="img-responsive block__projects__item__thumbnail" height="280" src="https://www.apc.org/sites/default/files/styles/350x350/public/CNimage_0.jpg?itok=29zc76s7" typeof="foaf:Image" width="350"/>
            </a>
            <a class="block__projects__item__title" href="/en/project/connecting-unconnected-supporting-community-networks-and-other-community-based-connectivity">
             Connecting the Unconnected: Supporting community networks and other community-based connectivity initiatives
            </a>
            <span class="block__latest_news__item__meta">
             <span>
              11 March 2019
             </span>
            </span>
            <p class="block__projects__item__excerpt">
            </p>
            <p>
             This project willcontribute to an enabling ecosystem for the emergence and growth of community networks and other community-based connectivity initiatives in developing countries. It is part of a multi-year, multi-donor strategy envisaged to address the human capacity and sustainability challenges, along with the policy and regulatory obstacles, that limit the growth of community-based connectivity initiatives.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="col-md-4">
           <div class="block__projects__item">
            <a href="/en/project/challenge">
             <img alt="Challenging hate narratives and violations of freedom of religion and expression online in Asia" class="img-responsive block__projects__item__thumbnail" height="280" src="https://www.apc.org/sites/default/files/styles/350x350/public/8331169181_979770c9cc_o_1.jpg?itok=aGQGaWuy" typeof="foaf:Image" width="350"/>
            </a>
            <a class="block__projects__item__title" href="/en/project/challenge">
             Challenging hate narratives and violations of freedom of religion and expression online in Asia
            </a>
            <span class="block__latest_news__item__meta">
             <span>
              18 December 2018
             </span>
            </span>
            <p class="block__projects__item__excerpt">
            </p>
            <p>
             This projectseeks to protect and promote respect for freedom of religion and expression on the internet, particularly by countering hate speech online on the basis of religion, and generating narratives and discourse that defend secular and diverse opinions touching upon religion.The three-year project focuses on five countries in South and Southeast Asia: Bangladesh, India, Indonesia, Myanmar and Pakistan.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="col-md-4">
           <div class="block__projects__item">
            <a href="/en/project/firn-feminist-internet-research-network">
             <img alt="FIRN: Feminist Internet Research Network" class="img-responsive block__projects__item__thumbnail" height="280" src="https://www.apc.org/sites/default/files/styles/350x350/public/IDRC-twitter_0.png?itok=b_x9d8nL" typeof="foaf:Image" width="350"/>
            </a>
            <a class="block__projects__item__title" href="/en/project/firn-feminist-internet-research-network">
             FIRN: Feminist Internet Research Network
            </a>
            <span class="block__latest_news__item__meta">
             <span>
              15 November 2018
             </span>
            </span>
            <p class="block__projects__item__excerpt">
            </p>
            <p>
             The Feminist Internet Research Network is a three-and-a-half-year collaborative and multidisciplinary research project led by APC, funded by the International Development Research Centre. The project draws on the study Mapping research in gender and digital technology, and the Feminist Principles of the Internet collectively crafted by feminists and activists, primarily located in the global South.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="col-md-4">
           <div class="block__projects__item">
            <a href="/en/projects/access/global-information-society-watch">
             <img alt="Global Information Society Watch" class="img-responsive block__projects__item__thumbnail" height="280" src="https://www.apc.org/sites/default/files/styles/350x350/public/DSC00710.JPG?itok=1sKwSSjk" typeof="foaf:Image" width="350"/>
            </a>
            <a class="block__projects__item__title" href="/en/projects/access/global-information-society-watch">
             Global Information Society Watch
            </a>
            <span class="block__latest_news__item__meta">
             <span>
              30 August 2010
             </span>
            </span>
            <p class="block__projects__item__excerpt">
            </p>
            <p>
             Global Information Society Watch (
             <span class="caps">
              GISW
             </span>
             atch) is an annual report co-produced by the
             <span class="caps">
              APC
             </span>
             network and partners, which looks at the progress being made in creating an inclusive information society worldwide (particularly in implementing
             <span class="caps">
              WSIS
             </span>
             goals), encourages critical debate, and strengthens networking and advocacy for a just, inclusive information society.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </section>
      <!-- /block__projects -->
     </section>

           </a>

             <a href="/en/blog/inside-digital-society-technological-disruption-and-complex-societies">
              <img alt="Inside the Digital Society: Technological disruption and complex societies" class="img-responsive block__latest_blog__item__thumbnail" height="280" src="https://www.apc.org/sites/default/files/styles/350x350/public/photo-1517895006477-9cfedb89a536.jpeg?itok=Y7hQBFmr" typeof="foaf:Image" width="350"/>

              <ul>
               <li>
                <a href="http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?s=100&amp;p[url]=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apc.org%2Fnode%2F37188&amp;p[title]=Inside+the+Digital+Society%3A+%C2%A0Technological+disruption+and+complex+societies&amp;p[images][0]=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apc.org%2Fsites%2Fdefault%2Ffiles%2Fphoto-1517895006477-9cfedb89a536.jpeg&amp;p[summary]=Technological+disruption+is+complex.+It+shouldn%E2%80%99t+just+be+understood+as+progress+or+as+threat.+There+will+be+winners+and+losers+from+it.%0A" target="_blank" title="Share on Facebook">
                 <img src="/sites/all/themes/apc2016/img/icons/orange-facebook.png"/>
                </a>
               </li>
               <li>
                <a href="http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?text=Inside+the+Digital+Society%3A+%C2%A0Technological+disruption+and+complex+societies&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apc.org%2Fnode%2F37188" target="_blank" title="Share on Twitter">
                 <img src="/sites/all/themes/apc2016/img/icons/orange-twitter.png"/>
                </a>
               </li>
              </ul>
             </div>
            </div>
           </a>
          </div>
          <div class="col-md-7 col-sm-7 col-custom-sm-7">
           <a class="block__apc_blog__item__title" href="">
           </a>
           <a class="block__apc_blog__item__title" href="/en/blog/inside-digital-society-technological-disruption-and-complex-societies">
            Inside the Digital Society: Technological disruption and complex societies
           </a>
           <span class="block__apc_blog__item__meta">
            <span>
             08 March 2021
            </span>
            <strong>
             David Souter
            </strong>
           </span>
           <p class="block__apc_blog__item__excerpt">
            Technological disruption is complex. It shouldnt just be understood as progress or as threat. There will be winners and losers from it.
           </p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <!-- yellow -->
      </div>
     </div>
    </section>
    <!-- /block__apc_blog -->
    <div class="region region-pre-content-3">
     <section class="block block-block columns-apc container clearfix" id="block-block-21">
      <h4 class="block-title">
       Columns
      </h4>
      <div style="margin-bottom: 45px;">
       <div class="photo">
        <img src="/sites/default/files/images/david-souter.jpg"/>
       </div>
       <p>
        <a href="/en/column/inside-information-society">
         Inside the Digital Society
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        David Souter writes a weekly column for APC, looking at different aspects of the information society, development and rights. Davids pieces take a fresh look at many of the issues that concern APC and its members, with the aim of provoking discussion and debate. Issues covered include internet governance and sustainable development, human rights and the environment, policy, practice and the use of ICTs by individuals and communities.
       </p>
      </div>
     </section>
     <section class="block block-views clearfix" id="block-views-publications-block">

              <a class="block__publications__item__title" href="/en/pubs/apc-comments-final-report-oewg-cybersecurity">

              </a>
              <p class="block__publications__item__excerpt">
               After two years of negotiations, the UN Open-ended Working Group (OEWG) on developments in the field of information and telecommunications in the context of international security has adopted its final report. Here, APC presents its positions on the most salient points of the report.
              </p>

              </a>
              <p class="block__publications__item__excerpt">
               APC welcomes the opportunity to engage in this session. We appreciate Ambassador Laubers openness to civil society and the OEWGs willingness to receive and consider comments by non-state actors.

              </a>
              <p class="block__publications__item__excerpt">

& Data","locality":"Bhaktapur","lat":27.6650737,"lng":85.4137044,"organisation":true,"url":"\/en\/member\/body-data"},{"name":"ASUTIC","locality":"Dakar","lat":14.71527778,"lng":-17.45722222,"organisation":true,"url":"\/en\/member\/asutic"}];

    var map = L.map('mapid', {
        center: [10.0, 5.0],
        minZoom: 2,
        zoom: 2
    });
    map.scrollWheelZoom.disable();
    map.zoomControl.setPosition('topright');

    L.tileLayer('http://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png', {}).addTo(map);


    var orgIcon = L.icon({
        iconUrl: '/sites/all/libraries/leaflet/images/map-Organisation.png',
        iconRetinaUrl: '/sites/all/libraries/leaflet/images/map-Organisation.png',
        iconSize: [21, 22],
        iconAnchor: [10, 22],
        popupAnchor: [10, 32]
    });
    var indIcon = L.icon({
        iconUrl: '/sites/all/libraries/leaflet/images/map-Individual.png',
        iconRetinaUrl: '/sites/all/libraries/leaflet/images/map-Individual.png',
        iconSize: [21, 31],
        iconAnchor: [10, 31],
        popupAnchor: [10, 41]
    });

    var markerClusters = L.markerClusterGroup();

    for (var i = 0; i < markers.length; ++i) {
        markers[i].locality = (!markers[i].locality) ? '' : markers[i].locality;
        var popup = '<div class="leaflet-popup-' + ((markers[i].organisation) ? 'organisation' : 'individual') + '-content">' +
            '<h1><a href="' + markers[i].url + '">' + markers[i].name + '</a></h1>' +
            '<div class="locality">' + markers[i].locality + '</div>' +
            '<div class="organisation-name"></div></div>';

        var icon = (markers[i].organisation) ? orgIcon : indIcon;

        var customOptions =
        {
            'maxWidth': '500',
            'className': 'custom'
        }
        var m = L.marker([markers[i].lat, markers[i].lng], {icon: icon}).bindPopup(popup, customOptions);

        markerClusters.addLayer(m);
    }

    map.addLayer(markerClusters);


    function redrawMapMarkers(orgs, inds) {
        markerClusters.clearLayers();

        for (var i = 0; i < markers.length; ++i) {
            if ((markers[i].organisation && orgs) || (!markers[i].organisation && inds)) {
                markers[i].locality = (!markers[i].locality) ? '' : markers[i].locality;
                var popup = '<div class="leaflet-popup-' + ((markers[i].organisation) ? 'organisation' : 'individual') + '-content">' +
                    '<h1><a href="' + markers[i].url + '">' + markers[i].name + '</a></h1>' +
                    '<div class="locality">' + markers[i].locality + '</div>' +
                    '<div class="organisation-name"></div></div>';

                var icon = (markers[i].organisation) ? orgIcon : indIcon;

                var m = L.marker([markers[i].lat, markers[i].lng], {icon: icon}).bindPopup(popup, customOptions);

                markerClusters.addLayer(m);
            }
        }
    }
      </script>

   </section>
